|  | Guideline for the use of the peer ranking form |  |  |  | HOTS5_1 |
| 1.0 | Fill in the ranking date in the table above. |  |  |  | HOTS5_2 |
| 2.0 | Fill in your project group name in the table above. |  |  |  | HOTS5_5 |
| 3.0 | Fill in the names of the group members in alphabetical sequence in the table above. |  |  |  | HOTS5_6 |
| 4.0 | Each student of the team must fill in the work page with the number that matches his or her name. |  |  |  | HOTS6_1 |
|  | Student 1 fills in work page / tab 1 for the corresponding week (3, 5 or 7) |  |  |  | HOTS6_2 |
|  | The student will grade all group members including himself or herself. |  |  |  | HOTS6_3 |
|  | A grade is a whole number (integer) from 1 until 10 |  |  |  | HOTS6_4 |
|  | 10 is maximal and means that the level meets the level of a young professional |  |  |  | HOTS6_5 |
|  | 1 is minimum and means there is very much to be improved |  |  |  | HOTS6_6 |
|  | Add relevant feedback on the line behind the grade, to facilitate reflection. |  |  |  | HOTS7_1 |
| 5.0 | You will fill the same form in during weeks 3, 5 and 7. |  |  |  |  |
|  | There is a separate column on each tab for each of these weeks. |  |  |  |  |
| 6.0 | Analyze for yourselves the individual averages sheet. The sheet provides insights in different competencies. |  |  |  | HOTS7_2 |
|  | Furthermore the sheet can help you compare your own impression of yourself to that of your team |  |  |  | HOTS7_3 |
| 7.0 | Share the group summary with your HOTS coach via email before the MT meeting. |  |  |  | HOTS7_4 |
|  |  |  |  |  | HOTS7_6 |
